 Netgear has recently launched a new router in India
 Orbi siries ke is router ko bijness customers ko torget karke dizin kiya gaya he
 It has a tri-band wifi system based on Netgear's Fastlane3 technology
 is router ke rivyuu main ham aapako bataange- Orbi Pro kii connactivity ke bare main, kya company ke daawey par khara utarataa he- dizin or bild quality kya isaki keemat ko jastiphai karata he- kya hai Orbi Pro ke khaas fitures- seoup kaise karen or yah kitna aasaan yaa mushkil he- spacifications ke bare mendizin or bild qualitylenetgtor Orbi Pro router ke box main do do divaais milte hai- base stesan router or satellite
 Both the design and build quality are of a kind and can be identified by the color coding given at the top of them
 rivyuu unit main router ke top par blue he jabaki satellite par grey diya gaya he
 The height of both is about 10 inches and their weight is less than 1 kg, so you can also call them portable
 inhen banane main hard plastic kaa yuj kiya gaya he
 Four ports are provided at the bottom in the rear of both devices
 donon main hi ek sinc or power batan diya gaya he
 Apart from this, DC port and reset option have been given
 router main teen ethernet port hai jabaki extander yani satellite divaais main chaar ethernet port (LAN) die gaye hai
 The router has an Internet (WAN) port to which you will place the cable provided by the Internet service provider
 aap router ko wal main mount kar sakate hai, isliye liye box main kit diya gaya he jise yuj kar sakate hai
 The user interface and setup router is very easy to setup and if you have an idea of your IP then you can setup it within 10 minutes
 power cabel or ethernet cord lagaana he iske baad satellite ko router se dur laga sakate hai ise bhi power kii jarurat hoti he
 The setup is similar to another router
 iske liye bhi aapako computer yaa mobile kii jarurat hogi
 By giving power to the device, you can scan your QR Code code on it and connect your smartphone to it
 haalanki iske baad aapako pehle seoup puraa karnaa hoga
 Wifi name and default password are written on the device, using which you can access the user interface
 baad main aap chahen to wifai kaa naam yani SSID or password badal sakate hai
 According to Netgear, Orbi Pro is designed specifically for small businesses that do not have dedicated IT personnel
 
 This router can provide connectivity speeds of up to 3gbps
 Orbi Pro router seoup puraa hone ke baad ye total teen wifai network banaate hai
 The first is an admin network that provides a network to the company
 isse aap apane bijness kaa printer or duusare sarvars jod sakate hai
 The second wifi network will be called Empoyee which is for staff
 isse mobile divaais or computer conect kar sakenge or yah phul acces hoga
 The third wifi SSID will be named Guest which will be for the guest users coming to the office
 isamen aap apane bijness yaa daftar kaa pej laga sakate hai jisamen company kaa naam or logo ho saktaa he
 It has limited use and it can be setup from the mobile app
 yah router chote bijness ke liye shandaar he, kyonki na sirf isaki kawarej jabardast he balki isamen die gaye fitures bhi ise khaas banaate hai
 If your business is small and cannot hire staff for IT then this is for you
 ise aap khud customij kar sakate hai or offis ke printers se lekar smartphone computer yaa sarwar se jod sakate hai
 This router can connect 40 users simultaneously and all can use internet simultaneously
 haalanki isse bhi zyada yugers jud to sakate hai, lekin phir bandwyeth alokeshan main dikkat hoti he is vajah se kinhin yugers ko connactivity main dikkaton kaa saamana karnaa pad saktaa he
 The coverage of this router is up to 5,000 square feet, which is enough for a small business
 testing ke dauraan hamane paaya he ki aakhri kawarej aria tak isaki connactivity jabardast rahati he or network chhootane jaisi samasya nahin hoti he
 The web interface of the router can be called quite difficult
